   sarvendriyāṇi saṃpratiṣṭhāpyāhiṃsan sarvabhūtāny anyatra tīrthebhyaḥ |	sarva-indriyANi saMpratizWApya-ahiMsan sarva-BUtAni anyatra tIrTeByaH |
   sa khalv evaṃ vartayan yāvad āyuṣaṃ brahmalokam abhisaṃpadyate |	sa Kalu evam vartayan yAvat Ayuzam brahma-lokam aBisaMpadyate |
   na ca punar āvartate na ca punar āvartate || ChUp_8,15.1 ||	na ca punar Avartate na ca punar Avartate || ShUp_8,15.1 ||
